 bataaya jaataa he ki baccha apane sambandhiyon ke paas he
 The accused can be produced in court on 3 July
 tippaniyan Joel Tucker, senior road safety consultant at the Royal Automobile Club, Queensland (RACQ), said that what happened was shocking
 unhone kaha, bacchon kii umr aisi nahin hoti ki vah car ko surakshit chalaa saken

 Bhawana Kanth, a flying officer of the Indian Air Force, has recorded his name in history by flying a plane plane
 aisa karne vaali vahabhartiya vaayu sena kii pehali mahila payalat ban gai hai
 Bhavna achieved this ability by successfully flying the Indian Flyer Plane mig-21
 bhaavana kii is uplabdhi par bhartiya vayusena ke captain or pravaktaa anupam banerjee ne kaha, 'bhaavana kanth ne din main fiter plane mig-21 (mig-21) ko udaakar is mishan ko puraa kiya
 She thus became the first Indian female fighter pilot to achieve this feat
 'bhaavana bhartiya vaayu sena ke pehle mahila fiter batch kii mahila fiter payalat he
 He was accompanied by two other female fighter pilots Avni Chaturvedi and Mohana Singh in 2016 as flying officers
 pehle vaayu sena main fiter payalat ke taur mahila payalton ke udaan kii anumati nahin thi
 In 2016, the then Defense Minister Manohar Parrikar had removed this rule and allowed women pilots to join the fighter air force as fighter pilots
 mig-21 (mig-21) bhartiya vaayu sena kaa sabase purana fiter plane he
 This plane was inducted into the Indian Air Force for the first time in 1964
 iske baad iselgataar aadhunik takneekon se apgrade kiya jaataa rahaa he
 The mig-21 is certainly a legacy of the Indian Air Force
 vartmaan main bhaavana rajastan ke bikaner sthit nal base par tainaat he
 Bhavana took the flight from Ambala Air Force Station in the Indian Air Force fighter plane mig-21 (bison)
 bhartiya vayusena ke ek adhikari ne kaha, 'ek baar vah raat ke mishan kaa prashikshan puraa kar len, to use raatri abhiyaan main bhi jane kii ijaajat di jaaegi
 Bhavna joined the fighter squadron in November 2017 and flown the mig-21 alone for the first time in March last year
 vaayu sena ke pravaktaa anupam banerjee ne kaha ki apni kadi mehnat or lagan ke kaaran vah is mukaam ko hasil karne vaali bhartiya vaayu sena kii pehali mahila adhikari bani hai

 salaami ballebaaj tameem ikbaal paanch, captain mushafikur rahim teen or nasir hossain ne ek ran banaae
 Mahmudullah (23) and Ziaur Rahman (26) returned unbeaten
 zimbabwe kii ore se greem krimar ne do jabaki bryan vittori, re price or alton chigumbura ne ek-ek wicket jhatka
 Earlier, Bangladesh won the toss and invited Zimbabwe to bat first
 zimbabwe ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah wicket par 134 ran banaae
 Vusi Sibanda scored the highest for Zimbabwe with 40 while captain Brendan Taylor contributed 21 and Craig Irwin contributed 19 runs
 hamiltan masakadja 12 or stuart maitsekenyari ne nau ran banaae
 Chigumbura (nine) and Creamer (0) returned unbeaten

 Sanjay Dutt has turned his film career towards a new path

 khabaron main bataaya ja rahaa he ki 'khalanaayak' main tiger shroff ko cast karne kii taiyaari he

 1993 main ai 'khalanaayak' (khalnayak) ko bollywood ke mashhoor diarector subhash ghai ne diarect kiya tha

 lekin hamane khalanaayak ke sikval ke adhikaron ko abhi nahin bechaa he

 unhone kaha, 'ham aashaa karte hai ki film ke ritis hamen mil jaaen

 andhra pradesh main wies jaganmohan reddy kii wiesar congress party (wiesarsipi) ne sattarudh congress or mukhya vipakshi telugu desham party (tedepa) ko jhatka dete hue shuukravaar ko nellore loksabhaa or 15 vidhansabha siton par kabja jamaa liya
 This by-election is being considered a semi-final of the 2014 general election
 divangat mukhyamantri wies rajasekhar reddy ke bete jagan ne wiesar congress party kaa gathan do varsh purv kiya tha
 The sympathy wave in favor of Jagan jailed in the disproportionate assets case was such that the ruling party had to satisfy only two assembly seats out of 18, while the main opposition tdp's account could not be opened
 jagan kii party ne tirupati vidhansabha seat bhi jeet lee he
 Karunakara Reddy, considered close to YSR, defeated the Congress candidate by 17,723 votes
 film abhinayta se rajaneta bane ke
 Chiranjeevi won the 2009 election from here
 unke rajyasabha ke liye chune jane se yah seat rikt ho gai thi
 Chief Minister N
 to remove Tirupati seat from Congress
 kiran kumaar reddy ke liye bada jhatka mana ja rahaa he
 This seat comes under his home district Chittoor
 12 jilon main faile 18 nirvachan kshetron main voton kii ginati kadi suraksha ke bich subah aath baje shuru hui
 In the by-elections held on Tuesday, Nellore recorded 70 percent of the vote and 80 percent of the assembly constituencies
 ek sansad sadsy ke istipha dene or congress se wiesarsipi main shaamil hone par 17 vidhayakon ko ayogy ghoshit kiye jane par upachunaavon kii sthiti paidaa hui thi
 In Nellore Lok Sabha constituency, ysrcp's Mekapati Rajamohan Reddy, his nearest rival, former Union Minister and Congress candidate T
K
 subbaraami reddy ko 290,000 se adhik maton ke antar se parajeet kiya
 The ruling Congress won two assembly seats and the Telangana Rashtra Samithi (TRS) got one
 chandrababu naidu kii tedepa kaa khaataa nahin khulaa
 The YSRCP has won 13 seats, which Congress won in 2009
 is party ne ek seat praja rajyam party (piarpy) se bhi chin lee he jiskaa ab congress main vilay ho chukaa he jabaki tiares ne congress se ek seat chhini he
 In this by-election, the Congress had to settle for only two seats
 uske liye yah apmanjanak sthiti he
 With these two seats, the number of Congress seats in the 294-member assembly will be 154
 rajya main bamushkil bahumat hasil karne vaali is party kii sthiti main isse thodaa sudhaar hoga
 TRS has barely won the Parkala assembly seat
 kade mukaable main tiares ummidavaar bheekshapati ne wiesarsipi kii konda surekha ko keval 800 maton se haraaya
 She was in fourth place until the 14th round of counting, but later made the TRS a bit difficult
 telugana kshetra ke keval paarkala vidhansabha kshetra main upachunaav hua tha
 The two top leaders to YSRCP p
 subhash chandra bose or konda surekha kii haar se jhatka laga he
 Both of them were ministers in Jagan's father ysr's cabinet
 subhash chandra bose ko purvi godavari jile ke ramchandrapuram nirvachan kshetra main shikast mili
 Congress candidate former minister K
 subbarayudu ne pashchimi godavari jile kii narsapuram seat jeet lee he
 The Congress won one seat each in East and West Godavari districts of coastal Andhra Pradesh, but lost to other seven seats in the region
 wiesarsipi ke pramukh vijetaon main bi
 Srinivas Reddy, Gurunath Reddy, Chenna Keshav Reddy, Srikanth Reddy and Dharmana Krishna Reddy
 shrinivas reddy vah wiesar parivaar ke ek rishtedaar hai or wiesar ke cabinet main mantri rah chuke hai
 YSRCP leader Jagan was arrested by the Central Bureau of Investigation (CBI) on May 27 in a disproportionate assets case
 us samay jagan apni party ke liye prachaar karne main vyast the
 His mother Vijayamma and sister Sharmila expressed their sympathy by accusing the Congress and TDP of targeting Jagan
 vijaymma ne do sitambar, 2009 ko helicopter durghatana main apane pati va tatkaaleen mukhyamantri wies rajasekhar reddy ke maare jane ke maamle main bhi congress kii ore ungali uthaakar sanshay jataayaa tha
 The comments saal 2010 ke aakhir main congress par parivaar todane kaa prayaas karne kaa aarope lagaate hue jagan ne kadappa loksabhaa seat va vijaymma ne pulivendula vidhansabha seat se istipha de diya tha
 He promised to implement the schemes launched by the YSR for the poor by forming YSRCP
 pichley saal hue upachunaavon main donon ne apni-apni pichhali siton par dobaaraa baari bahumat se jeet hasil kii
 The YSRCP also won the Kovur Assembly seat in Nellore district, vacated by the resignation of the TDP MLA, in the by-election held in March this year

 subbaraami reddy ko 290,000 se adhik maton ke antar se parajeet kiya
 The ruling Congress won two assembly seats and the Telangana Rashtra Samithi (TRS) got one
 chandrababu naidu kii tedepa kaa khaataa nahin khulaa
 The YSRCP has won 13 seats, which Congress won in 2009
 is party ne ek seat praja rajyam party (piarpy) se bhi chin lee he jiskaa ab congress main vilay ho chukaa he jabaki tiares ne congress se ek seat chhini he
 In this by-election, the Congress had to settle for only two seats
 uske liye yah apmanjanak sthiti he
 With these two seats, the number of Congress seats in the 294-member assembly will be 154
 rajya main bamushkil bahumat hasil karne vaali is party kii sthiti main isse thodaa sudhaar hoga
 TRS has barely won the Parkala assembly seat
 kade mukaable main tiares ummidavaar bheekshapati ne wiesarsipi kii konda surekha ko keval 800 maton se haraaya
 She was in fourth place until the 14th round of counting, but later made the TRS a bit difficult
 telugana kshetra ke keval paarkala vidhansabha kshetra main upachunaav hua tha
 The two top leaders to YSRCP p
 subhash chandra bose or konda surekha kii haar se jhatka laga he
 Both of them were ministers in Jagan's father ysr's cabinet
 subhash chandra bose ko purvi godavari jile ke ramchandrapuram nirvachan kshetra main shikast mili
 Congress candidate former minister K
 subbarayudu ne pashchimi godavari jile kii narsapuram seat jeet lee he
 The Congress won one seat each in East and West Godavari districts of coastal Andhra Pradesh, but lost to other seven seats in the region
 wiesarsipi ke pramukh vijetaon main bi
 Srinivas Reddy, Gurunath Reddy, Chenna Keshav Reddy, Srikanth Reddy and Dharmana Krishna Reddy
 shrinivas reddy vah wiesar parivaar ke ek rishtedaar hai or wiesar ke cabinet main mantri rah chuke hai
 YSRCP leader Jagan was arrested by the Central Bureau of Investigation (CBI) on May 27 in a disproportionate assets case
 us samay jagan apni party ke liye prachaar karne main vyast the
 His mother Vijayamma and sister Sharmila expressed their sympathy by accusing the Congress and TDP of targeting Jagan
 vijaymma ne do sitambar, 2009 ko helicopter durghatana main apane pati va tatkaaleen mukhyamantri wies rajasekhar reddy ke maare jane ke maamle main bhi congress kii ore ungali uthaakar sanshay jataayaa tha
 The comments saal 2010 ke aakhir main congress par parivaar todane kaa prayaas karne kaa aarope lagaate hue jagan ne kadappa loksabhaa seat va vijaymma ne pulivendula vidhansabha seat se istipha de diya tha
 He promised to implement the schemes launched by the YSR for the poor by forming YSRCP
 pichley saal hue upachunaavon main donon ne apni-apni pichhali siton par dobaaraa baari bahumat se jeet hasil kii
 The YSRCP also won the Kovur Assembly seat in Nellore district, vacated by the resignation of the TDP MLA, in the by-election held in March this year
 nellore loksabhaa nirvachan kshetra main wiesarsipi ke mekapati rajamohan reddy ne apane nakatatam pratidwandvi purv kendriya mantri evam congress pratyaashee tii
 Subbarami Reddy was defeated by a margin of over 290,000 votes
 sattarudh congress ne do vidhansabha siten jiti hai or telugana raashtra samiti (tiares) ko ek seat mili he
 Chandrababu Naidu's account of TDP did not open
 wiesarsipi ne ve 13 siten jeet lee hai jin par 2009 main congress ne kabja jamaaya tha
 This party has also wrested one seat from Praja Rajyam Party (PRP) which has now been merged with Congress while TRS has wrested one seat from Congress
 is upachunaav main congress ko keval do siton se santosh karnaa padaa he
 It is a humiliating situation for him
 in do siton se 294 sadasyeey vidhansabha main congress kii siton kii sankhya 154 ho jaaegi
 This party, which barely gets a majority in the state, will improve a bit
 tiares ko paarkala vidhansabha seat par mushkil se jeet mili he
 In the tough contest, TRS candidate Bhishkapati defeated Konda Surekha of YSRCP by only 800 votes
 14wein daur kii matganana tak vah chauthe sthaan par thim, lekin baad main unhone tiares kii raah thodi mushkil kar di
 The bypoll was held in only the Parakala assembly constituency of Telangana region
 wiesarsipi ko do sheersh netaaon pi
 Subhash Chandra Bose and Konda Surekha have suffered a setback
 ye donon jagan ke pita wiesar ke mantrimandal main mantri rah chuke the
 Subhash Chandra Bose was defeated in Ramachandrapuram constituency in East Godavari district
 congress ummidavaar purv mantri ke
 Subbarayudu has won Narasapuram seat in West Godavari district
 congress ne tateey andhra pradesh kii purvi or pashchimi godavari jile kii ek-ek seat jiti he lekin kshetra kii anya saat siton par use karaari haar mili
 B
 among the major winners of YSRCP
 shrinivas reddy, gurunath reddy, chenna keshav reddy, shrikant reddy or dharmana krishna reddy shaamil hai
 Srinivasa Reddy He is a relative of the YSR family and has been a minister in the YSR cabinet
 wiesarsipi netaa jagan ko kendriya jaanch beuro (sibiai) ne aay se adhik sampatti ke maamle main 27 may ko giraftaar kiya tha
 At that time Jagan was busy campaigning for his party
 unki maa vijaymma va bahan sharmila ne congress va tedepa par jagan ko nishaanaa banane kaa aarope lagaakar logon kii sahanubhuti batori
 Vijayamma also raised doubts about the Congress by raising her finger in the case of the killing of her husband and the then Chief Minister YS Rajasekhara Reddy in a helicopter crash on September 2, 2009
 tippaniyan In late 2010, Jagan resigned from Kadapa Lok Sabha seat and Vijayamma from Pulivendula assembly seat, accusing the Congress of trying to break up the family
 unhone wiesarsipi kaa gathan kar wiesar dwaara garibon ke liye shuru kii gai yojanaayen lagu karne kaa vaada kiya
 In the by-elections held last year, both of them won their previous seats again by a huge majority

 Subrata Roy, the head of the Sahara Group, embroiled in a heated dispute with market regulator Sebi, feels that he has been harassed for the past few years and started with the political malice incident in 2005 and against the Reserve Bank and Sebi companies Shinkaja started tightening
 gauratlab he ki samooh kii do companiyon ke niveshkon kaa kareeb 24,000 karod rupee waapas karne ke maamle main unke vyaktigat or company kii sampattiyon kii sebi dwaara nilaamee karaae jane kaa khatra utpann ho gaya he
 Subrata Roy was summoned in this case at Sebi headquarters in Mumbai on Wednesday
 roy ne pitiai ke saath phone par baatcheet main kaha, isaki shuruyaat 2005 main hamaare khilaaf ek raajnneetik dwesh ke saath hui or uske baad se ek silsilaa chal padaa
 First the Reserve Bank took action against us in 2008, after which SEBI clamped down on our companies
 sahaara samooh vividh prakaar ke vyavsaay main laga he, jisamen manoranjan se lekar jameen-jaaydaad ke vikaas, tathaa vittiya sevaaon se lekar hotel tak kaa kaarobaar shaamil hai
 Roy said that due to the action of Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI), the business of his other companies is being affected
 baavjood iske roy ne kaha ki vah 'aakhri dam' tak ladenge
 He expressed confidence that the matter would be resolved at the appropriate time
 sebi ne roy or unke teen sahyogiyon ko unki or sahaara samooh kii do companiyon - esaiaraisiel or esechasiiel - kii sampattiyon kii pushti ke liye buudhvaar ko apane mukhyalay main bulaayaa tha, taaki in sampattiyon kii nilaamee ke jariye dhan jutakar niveshkon kaa paisa lautaaya ja sake
 The comments sebi kaa aarope he ki esaiaraisiel or esechasiiel ne band dharakon se 6,380 karod rupee or 19,400 karod rupee jutaaye the, lekin dhan jutaney ke liye kai tarah kii aniyamitatayen kii gayi
 The Supreme Court has ordered the refund of the money of more than three crore bond holders of these companies and the work of returning the money has been given to SEBI after verifying the investors
 apni baat par kaayam subrat roy kaa daawa he ki rigerv bank or sebi ke kuch adhikari nijee khunnas ke kaaran unke company samooh ko nishaanaa banaae hue hai
 He said that in the last two years, 60 percent of his time was spent fighting SEBI, which could be utilized in constructive work
 unhone kaha, is kaaran hamen bahut nuksaan hua he
 When asked if he is feeling harassed, he said, "we are definitely being harassed
" sebi hamen akaaran hi nishane par rakhe hue he
 Significantly, in the matter of returning the investors of the two companies of the group to the tune of about Rs 24,000 crore, there is a risk of their personal and company assets being auctioned by SEBI
 subrat roy ko is maamle main buudhvaar ko mumbai main sebi ke mukhyalay par talab kiya gaya tha
 In a phone conversation with PTI, Roy said, "it started in 2005 with a political malice against us and since then there has been a series
" pehle rigerv bank ne 2008 main hamaare khilaaf karrwai kii, uske baad sebi ne hamaari companiyon par shikanje chadha die
 The Sahara Group is engaged in a wide variety of businesses, ranging from entertainment to real estate development, and financial services to hotels
 roy ne kaha ki bhartiya pratibhuti evam vinimay board (sebi) kii karrwai ke chalate unki anya companiyon ke kaarobaar par asar pad rahaa he

 unhone vishwaas jataayaa ki uchit samay par maamla sulajhaa liya jayega
 SEBI had summoned Roy and his three associates at their headquarters on Wednesday to verify the assets of them and two Sahara Group companies - SIRECL and SHCIL - to raise funds through auction of these assets and return investors' money
 tippaniyan SEBI alleges that SIRECL and SHCIL raised Rs 6,380 crore and Rs 19,400 crore from the bond holders, but a number of irregularities were done to raise funds
 supreme court ne in companiyon ke teen karod se adhik band dharakon kaa paisa lautaane kaa aadesh de rakhaa he or niveshkon kaa satyaapan karte hue paisa lautwane kaa kaam sebi ko diya gaya he
 Subrata Roy maintains that some officials of the Reserve Bank and Sebi are targeting his group of companies due to private mines
 unhone kaha ki pichley do saal main unka 60 pratishat samay sebi se ladane main jaaya hua, jiskaa sadupyog rachanaatmak kaary main ho saktaa tha
 He said, we have suffered a lot due to this
 yah puche jane par bhi ki kya ve pratadit mahasoos kar rahe hai, unhone kaha, nishchit taur par hamen pratadit kiya ja rahaa he

 Uploading these figures, the EPFO has said that the figures for recent months are provisional
 karmchaariyon ke record kaa adhyatan ek satat prakriya he

 ipiefo ne kaha ki yah aayu varg ke hisaab se aankada sabhi gaiyr shunya yogadanakartaaon kaa he , jo sambandhit maheene main ipiefo ke tahat panjikrut hue hai

 uske baad yah palat gai

 jila or police ke varisht adhikariyon ne ghatnasthal par shivi lagaakar padaav daal rakhaa he or bachaav kaaryon kaa jayja le rahe hai
 The neighboring country of Pakistan is celebrating the 15th birthday of its Atom bomb today
 is salanaa utsav ko 'yom e takabeer' kaa naam diya gaya he
 May 28, 1998, this day Pakistan considers its date as special, because according to it, the world's first Islamic bomb was prepared on this day
 is daawey ke peeche kaa tark he, aisa pehla muslim desh hona, jisane atom bam kaa test kiya ho

 islamic bam ke janak maane jane vaale newclear scientist kaadir khan ko bhi baad main nirvaasan or jail bhugatni padi thi

 iske kuch maheenon baad bharat or pakistan ke bich nae sire se shanti vaarta shuru hui thi or phir 1999 main vaajapeyi bas par savaar hokar lahore gaye the

 match se pehle darshakon kaa khyalgavaskar ne kaha, ‘bharat-pakistan match se pehle bhavanaaen kaaphi ufaan par rahati hai
 Whatever Shahid said, it was a good way to say good things about the Indian audience
 eden garden par darshak pakistan ke prati virdohi nahin honge
 'the effect of the audience's emotions' said Gavaskar,' The emotions of the audience have a lot of effect, you play according to the audience
 eden ke darshakon ko jeetne kaa yahi acha tarika he

 ’puure dil se khelte the miyandadamiyandad kii pratikriya ke bare main poochne par gavaskar ne kaha, ‘yah har insaan par nirbhar karata he
 "he said," When Miandad played for Pakistan, he used to play whole heartedly
 jab vah bharat ke khilaaf khelte, to vah apana 200 pratishat dete the
 He always had an invisible flag with him
 isliye vah shahid se khafa ho gaye

 The company admitted that its business was affected by the lack of new models
 company kii nai hazbek 'bolt' or nai kampact sedan 'jest' is calendar varsh kii duusari chamahi main bazaar main aegi or company ne apni 2020 utpaada yojana ke tahat bazaar main pehle jaisi sthiti hasil karne kii taiyaari kii he
